   udgṛhṇīdhvaṃ mārṣā imaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ sarvakarmāvaraṇakleśakṣayaṃkaraṃ	udgRhNIDvam mArzAH imam Darma-paryAyam sarva-karma-AvaraNa-kleSa-kzayaMkaram
   yasya paścātkāle śravaṇamātreṇāpi sattvānāṃ sarvakarmāvaraṇakleśakṣayo	yasya paScAt-kAle SravaNa-mAtreNa-api sattvAnAm sarva-karma-AvaraNa-kleSa-kzayaH-
   bhaviṣyati // idam avocad bhagavān / āttamanā sā ca sarvāvatī parṣat	Bavizyati // idam avocat BagavAn / Atta-manA sA ca sarvAvatI parzad-
   sadevamānuṣāsuragandharvaś ca loko bhagavato bhāṣitam abhyanandat // //	sa-deva-mAnuza-asura-ganDarvaH ca lokaH BagavataH BAzitam aByanandat // //
   mahāsannipātān mahāyānasūtrād ratnaketuniṣṭhāgamaparivartas trayodaśamaḥ	mahAsannipAtAt mahAyAna-sUtrAt ratna-ketu-nizWA-gama-parivartaH trayodaSamaH
   samāptāḥ // //	samAptAH // //

   saṃskṛtvā ratnaketuṃ pracurabhayaharān dhāraṇīṃ yan mayāgryaṃ	saMskRtvA ratnaketum pracura-Baya-harAn DAraNIm yat mayA-agryam
   puṇyaṃ kiṃcit prasūtaṃ pramuditamanasā sarvabhaktyādṛtena /	puNyam kiMcid prasUtam pramudita-manasA sarva-Bakti-AdRtena /
   sarvo 'yaṃ tena loko munivacanakathālaṃkṛtāṃ ratnaketuṃ hy	sarvaH ayam tena lokaH muni-vacana-kaTA-alaMkRtAm ratnaketum hi-
   etām eva sphuṭārthām atiguṇaviśadāṃ prāpnuyāt sadya eva : // //	etAm eva sPuwa-arTAm ati-guNa-viSadAm prApnuyAt sadyas eva : // //
   saddharmasaṃgraho śrīpaṭolaṣāhi vikramādityanandasy śrīmahādevyāṃ	sadDarma-saMgrahaH SrI-pawolazAhi vikramAdityanandasi SrI-mahAdevyAm
   surendramālāyāṃ tathā sārdhaṃ uvakhī śrīmahādevyāṃ dilnitapuṇyāṃ // tathā	sura-indra-mAlAyAm taTA sArDam uvaKI SrI-mahAdevyAm dilnita-puNyAm // taTA
   sārdhaṃ pustakalikhāpitam idaṃ mahādānapatim etalagor nikṣiṇasya tathā	sArDam pusta-kali-KApitam idam mahA-dAna-patim etalagoH nikziNasya taTA
   sārdhaṃ bhāryā āśṇāti kasumo.valtāyāṃ tathā sārdhaṃ mātā aspinaśūlāyāṃ //	sArDam BAryA ASNAti kasumo.valtAyAm taTA sArDam mAtA aspina-SUlAyAm //
